<script type="text/javascript">
  window.onload = function() {
    const accessibilityLinkContainer = document.getElementById("accessibilityLinkContainer");
    switch(window.navigator.language) {
      case "fr":
        if (accessibilityLinkContainer != null) {
          const accessibilityText="Accessibilité : partiellement conforme";
          const frenchAccessibilityAnchor = document.createElement("a");
          frenchAccessibilityAnchor.id = "frenchAccesssibleLink";
          frenchAccessibilityAnchor.target = "_blank";
          frenchAccessibilityAnchor.href = "https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=2163806";
          frenchAccessibilityAnchor.title = accessibilityText;
          frenchAccessibilityAnchor.innerText = accessibilityText;
          accessibilityLinkContainer.appendChild(frenchAccessibilityAnchor);
        }
        break;
      case "it":
        if (accessibilityLinkContainer != null) {
          const accessibilityText="Accessibilità: parzialmente conforme";
          const italianAccessibilityAnchor = document.createElement("a");
          italianAccessibilityAnchor.id = "italianAccesssibleLink";
          italianAccessibilityAnchor.target = "_blank";
          italianAccessibilityAnchor.href = "https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=2208177";
          italianAccessibilityAnchor.title = accessibilityText;
          italianAccessibilityAnchor.innerText = accessibilityText;
          accessibilityLinkContainer.appendChild(italianAccessibilityAnchor);
        }
        break;
      default: 
        accessibilityLinkContainer.remove();
    }
  };

	<script type="text/javascript">

        function trackCopilotCustomUsage(botSchema) {
            const request = {
                botSchemaName: botSchema
            }
            var json = JSON.stringify(request);
            shell.ajaxSafePost({
                type: "POST",
                contentType: "application/json",
                url: "/_services/copilot/TrackUsage",
                data: json
            }).done(function () {
            }).fail(function (jqXhr) {
            });
        }

        function findAndLogCustomCopilotUsage() {
            const pageSource = document.documentElement.outerHTML;
            const customPvaBotWebchatRegex = /api\.(preprod\.|test\.)?powerplatform\.(com|us|cn|appsplatform\.us)\/powervirtualagents\/botsbyschema\/([^/]+)\/directline\/token/;
            const customPvaBotIframeRegex = /powerva\.microsoft\.com\/environments\/([0-9a-fA-F\-]+)\/bots\/([^/]+)\/webchat/;
            const omniChannelRegex = /livechatwidget\/scripts\/LiveChatBootstrapper\.js/;

            const matchPvaBotWebchat = pageSource.match(customPvaBotWebchatRegex);
            if (matchPvaBotWebchat && matchPvaBotWebchat[3]) {
                trackCopilotCustomUsage(matchPvaBotWebchat[3]);
            }

            const matchPvaBotIframe = pageSource.match(customPvaBotIframeRegex);
            if (matchPvaBotIframe && matchPvaBotIframe[2]) {
                trackCopilotCustomUsage(matchPvaBotIframe[2]);
            }

            const matchOmniChannel = pageSource.match(omniChannelRegex);
            if (matchOmniChannel && matchOmniChannel[0]) {
                trackCopilotCustomUsage("omnichannelWidget");
            }
        }

        window.addEventListener("load", function () {
            findAndLogCustomCopilotUsage();
        });
    </script>

<script>
  function checkUserSession() {
    
    var userExists = false;
    

    if (userExists) {
      checkLastLogin();
    }
  }

  function checkLastLogin() {
    var lastLogin = localStorage.getItem('last_login');
    if (lastLogin === null) {
      localStorage.setItem('last_login', new Date().toISOString());
    } else {
      var lastLoginDate = new Date(lastLogin);
      var currentDate = new Date();

      var timeDifference = currentDate - lastLoginDate;
      var hoursDifference = timeDifference / (1000 * 60 * 60);

      if (hoursDifference >= 9) {
        console.log(3); // This will print '3' to the console, you can replace this with appropriate action
        localStorage.clear();
        window.location.href = '/Account/Login/LogOff?returnUrl=/';
      }
    }
  }

  // Check session and last login immediately
  checkUserSession();

  // Set intervals for checking user session and last login regularly
  setInterval(checkUserSession, 600000); // Check session every 10 minutes
  setInterval(checkLastLogin, 20 * 60 * 1000); // Check login status every 20 minutes

  window.tabletCheck = function() { 
    const width = window.innerWidth;
    return width >= 767 && width <= 1024;
  }

  if (tabletCheck()) {
    document.getElementById('mainContent').classList.add('tablet');

    window.mobileCheck = function () {
      const width = window.innerWidth;
      return width <= 768;
    };

    function generalLogOut() {
    localStorage.clear();
    sessionStorage.clear();
    const portalUrl = window.location.hostname;
    window.location.href =
      portalUrl + "/Account/Login/LogOff?returnUrl=%2F%3FcompleteLogOut%3Dtrue";
  }

    window.texts = {};

    fetch('/web-pages/request/content-pages/texts.json')
    .then(res => res.json())
    .then(data => {
        console.log('data ', data);

        window.texts = data;
      });

    window.getText = function (path, fallback = '') {
      if (!window.texts) return fallback;
      return path.split('.').reduce((obj, key) => (obj && obj[key] !== undefined ? obj[key] : undefined), window.texts) ?? fallback;
    };

    (function (webapi, $) {
      function safeAjax(ajaxOptions) {
        var deferredAjax = $.Deferred();

        shell.getTokenDeferred().done(function (token) {
          // add headers for AJAX
          if (!ajaxOptions.headers) {
            $.extend(ajaxOptions, {
              headers: {
                "__RequestVerificationToken": token
              }
            });
          } else {
            ajaxOptions.headers["__RequestVerificationToken"] = token;
          }
          $.ajax(ajaxOptions)
            .done(function (data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
              validateLoginSession(data, textStatus, jqXHR, deferredAjax.resolve);
            }).fail(deferredAjax.reject); //AJAX
        }).fail(function () {
          deferredAjax.rejectWith(this, arguments); // on token failure pass the token AJAX and args
        });

        return deferredAjax.promise();
      }
      webapi.safeAjax = safeAjax;
    })(window.webapi = window.webapi || {}, jQuery);

    const saveToSession = (key, data) => {
      sessionStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(data));
    }

    const loadFromSession = (key) => {
      try {
        const data = sessionStorage.getItem(key);
        return data ? JSON.parse(data) : null;
      } catch (error) {
        console.error(`Error parsing JSON for key "${key}":`, error);
        return null;
      }
    };

    function groupAndSort(list, key, isFormatted) {
      const index = isFormatted ? 1 : 0;
      const grouped = list.reduce((acc, item) => {
        const TypeCode = item[key]?.split(' - ')[index]?.trim();
        if (!TypeCode) return acc;

        if (!acc[TypeCode]) {
          acc[TypeCode] = [];
        }

        acc[TypeCode].push(item);
        return acc;
      }, {});

      // מיון לפי השדה order
      for (const TypeCode in grouped) {
        grouped[TypeCode].sort((a, b) => a.order - b.order);
      }
      return grouped;
    }

    function getStatusByCode(guid) {
      const defaultStatus = {
        id: -1,
        name: "סטטוס לא ידוע",
        description: "אין מידע על סטטוס זה",
        color: { border: '1px #E2E2E2 solid', backgroundColor: 'white', color: '#626262' },
        num_code: -1,
        num_code_formatted: "לא ידוע",
        p_record_state_code: -1,
        p_record_state_code_formatted: "לא ידוע"
      };

      if (typeof statusMap !== 'undefined' && Array.isArray(statusMap)) {
        const result = statusMap.find(s => s.id === guid);
        return result || defaultStatus;
      }
      const statusFromSession = loadFromSession("status");
      if (Array.isArray(statusFromSession)) {
        const result = statusFromSession.find(s => s.id === guid);
        return result || defaultStatus;
      }


      return defaultStatus;
    }

    function getClassificationByCode(guid) {
      const defaultClassification = {
        id: -1,
        name: "סיווג לא ידוע",
        description: "אין מידע על סיווג זה"
      };

      if (typeof classificationsMap !== 'undefined' && Array.isArray(classificationsMap)) {
        const result = classificationsMap.find(c => c.id === guid);
        return result || defaultClassification;
      }
      const classificationsFromSession = loadFromSession("classifications");
      if (Array.isArray(classificationsFromSession)) {
        const result = classificationsFromSession.find(s => s.id === guid);
        return result || defaultClassification;
      }
      return defaultClassification;
    }

    const directTo = (path, params = {}) => {
      const homePage = window.location.origin;
      const queryString = Object.entries(params)
        .filter(([_, value]) => value !== undefined && value !== null && value !== "")
        .map(([key, value]) => `${encodeURIComponent(key)}=${encodeURIComponent(value)}`)
        .join("&");

      const fullUrl = `${homePage}/${path}/` + (queryString ? `?${queryString}` : "");
      window.location.href = fullUrl;
    };



    function Data({ setDataLoaded, requiredKeys = ["status", "classifications", "orefCitiesData", "fields"] }) {

      function safeGet(url, select) {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
          webapi.safeAjax({
            type: "GET",
            url: `${url}?$select=${select}`,
            contentType: "application/json",
            headers: {
              "Prefer": "odata.include-annotations=*"
            },
            success: resolve,
            error: reject
          });
        });
      }

      async function getStatus() {
        const sessionKey = "status";
        const prevData = loadFromSession(sessionKey);
        if (prevData) return prevData;

        const fetchPromise = safeGet("/_api/oref_statuses", [
          "oref_statusid",
          "oref_p_record_state_code",
          "oref_color",
          "oref_num_code",
          "oref_name",
          "oref_description",
          "oref_label",
          "oref_is_fields_editable"
        ].join(','));

        // const isRequired = requiredKeys.includes(sessionKey);
        // const data = isRequired ? await fetchPromise : undefined;
        const data =await fetchPromise;

        if (!data) return;

        const status = data.value.map(item => ({
          id: item["oref_statusid"],
          name: item["oref_name"],
          description: item["oref_description"],
          label: item["oref_label"],
          color: JSON.parse(item["oref_color"]),
          num_code: item["oref_num_code"],
          num_code_formatted: item["oref_num_code@OData.Community.Display.V1.FormattedValue"],
          p_record_state_code: item["oref_p_record_state_code"],
          p_record_state_code_formatted: item["oref_p_record_state_code@OData.Community.Display.V1.FormattedValue"],
          is_fields_editable: item["oref_is_fields_editable"],
          is_fields_editable_formatted: item["oref_is_fields_editable@OData.Community.Display.V1.FormattedValue"],
        }));

        window.statusMap = status;
        saveToSession(sessionKey, status);
        return status;
      }

      async function getClassifications() {
        const sessionKey = "classifications";
        const prevData = loadFromSession(sessionKey);
        if (prevData) return prevData;

        const fetchPromise = safeGet("/_api/oref_incident_classifications", [
          "oref_incident_classificationid",
          "oref_p_request_entity",
          "oref_message_text_for_submitted_status",
          "oref_closure_message",

          "oref_pdf_link",

          "oref_description",
          "oref_image_no_requests",
          "oref_image_with_requests"
        ].join(','));

        // const isRequired = requiredKeys.includes(sessionKey);
        // const data = isRequired ? await fetchPromise : undefined;
        const data =await fetchPromise;

        if (!data) return;

        const classifications = data.value.map(result => ({
          id: result["oref_incident_classificationid"],
          num_code: result["oref_num_code"],
          num_code_formatted: result["oref_num_code@OData.Community.Display.V1.FormattedValue"],
          name: result["oref_name"],
          description: result["oref_description"],
          p_request_entity: result["oref_p_request_entity"],
          p_request_entity_formatted: result["oref_p_request_entity@OData.Community.Display.V1.FormattedValue"],
          message_text_for_submitted_status: result["oref_message_text_for_submitted_status"],
          submit_request_pop_up_text: result["oref_submit_request_pop_up_text"],
          closure_message: result["oref_closure_message"],
          num_status_change_rule_code: result["oref_num_status_change_rule_code"],
          image_no_requests: result["oref_image_no_requests"],
          image_with_requests: result["oref_image_with_requests"],
          pdf_link: result["oref_pdf_link"],
        }));

        window.classificationsMap = classifications;
        saveToSession(sessionKey, classifications);
        return classifications;
      }

      async function getFields() {
        const sessionKey = "fields";
        const prevData = loadFromSession(sessionKey);
        if (prevData) return prevData;

        const fetchPromise = safeGet("/_api/oref_page_content_managements", [
          "oref_page_content_managementid",
          "oref_error_message",
          "oref_validation",
          "_oref_form_type_id_value",
          "oref_name",
          "oref_form_name",
          "oref_form_field_label",
          "oref_num_order",
          "oref_field_type",
          "oref_field_options"
        ].join(','));

        // const isRequired = requiredKeys.includes(sessionKey);
        // const data = isRequired ? await fetchPromise : undefined;
        const data =await fetchPromise;

        if (!data) return;

        const results = data.value.map(result => ({
          id: result["oref_page_content_managementid"],
          validation: result["oref_validation"],
          error_message: result["oref_error_message"],
          form_type_id: result["_oref_form_type_id_value"],
          form_type_id_formatted: result["_oref_form_type_id_value@OData.Community.Display.V1.FormattedValue"],

          form_field_label: result["oref_form_field_label"],
          order: result["oref_num_order"],
          type: result["oref_field_type"],
          options: result["oref_field_options"],
        }));

        saveToSession(sessionKey, results);
        return results;
      }

      async function fetchOrefCities() {
        const sessionKey = "orefCitiesData";
        const prevData = loadFromSession(sessionKey);
        if (prevData) return prevData;

        const fetchPromise = safeGet("/_api/oref_cities", [
          "oref_cityid",
          "oref_num_code",
          "oref_name",
          "oref_description"
        ].join(','));

        // const isRequired = requiredKeys.includes(sessionKey);
        // const data = isRequired ? await fetchPromise : undefined;
        const data =await fetchPromise;

        if (!data) return;

        const mappedResults = data.value.map(item => ({
          id: item["oref_cityid"],
          code: item["oref_num_code"],
          codeFormatted: item["oref_num_code@OData.Community.Display.V1.FormattedValue"] || null,
          name: item["oref_name"],
          description: item["oref_description"]
        }));

        saveToSession(sessionKey, mappedResults);
        return mappedResults;
      }

      function fetchRequiredDocuments() {
        const sessionKey = "requiredDocuments";
        const prevData = loadFromSession(sessionKey);
        if (prevData) return prevData;
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
          webapi.safeAjax({
            type: "GET",
            url: `/_api/oref_case_required_documents?$select=oref_case_required_documentid,oref_p_required,oref_num_max_file_count,_oref_document_type_id_value,oref_p_file_type,_oref_incident_classification_id_value&$expand=oref_document_type_id($select=oref_num_code,oref_name,oref_description)&$filter=_oref_incident_classification_id_value eq ${window.OREF_CONFIG.CLASSIFICATIONS.PERMIT}`,
            contentType: "application/json",
            headers: {
              "Prefer": "odata.include-annotations=*"
            },
            success: function (data) {
              const results = data.value.map(result => ({
                id: result["oref_case_required_documentid"],
                isRequired: {
                  value: result["oref_p_required"],
                  label: result["oref_p_required@OData.Community.Display.V1.FormattedValue"]
                },
                maxFileCount: {
                  value: result["oref_num_max_file_count"],
                  label: result["oref_num_max_file_count@OData.Community.Display.V1.FormattedValue"]
                },
                fileTypes: {
                  value: result["oref_p_file_type"],
                  label: result["oref_p_file_type@OData.Community.Display.V1.FormattedValue"]
                },
                documentType: {
                  id: result["_oref_document_type_id_value"],
                  name: result["_oref_document_type_id_value@OData.Community.Display.V1.FormattedValue"],
                  title: result?.oref_document_type_id?.oref_name,
                  description: result?.oref_document_type_id?.oref_description,
                  code: result?.oref_document_type_id?.oref_num_code
                },
                incidentClassification: {
                  id: result["_oref_incident_classification_id_value"],
                  name: result["_oref_incident_classification_id_value@OData.Community.Display.V1.FormattedValue"],
                  entity: result["_oref_incident_classification_id_value@Microsoft.Dynamics.CRM.lookuplogicalname"]
                }
              }));

              // Sort results by oref_num_code
              results.sort((a, b) => {
                const codeA = a.documentType.code || 0;
                const codeB = b.documentType.code || 0;
                return codeA - codeB;
              });

              saveToSession(sessionKey, results); // Fixed variable name from mappedResults to results
              resolve(results);
            },
            error: function (xhr, textStatus, errorThrown) {
              reject({ xhr, textStatus, errorThrown });
            }
          });
        });
      }

      async function fetchPermitRequestTypes() {

      }

      function MessagesList({ messages }) {
        const [showAll, setShowAll] = React.useState(false);
        const INITIAL_DISPLAY_COUNT = 4;

        const displayedMessages = showAll ? messages : messages.slice(0, INITIAL_DISPLAY_COUNT);
        const hasMoreMessages = messages.length > INITIAL_DISPLAY_COUNT;

        return (
          <div className="messages-list">
            {displayedMessages.map((message, index) => (
              <div key={index} className="message-item">
                <p className="message-title">{message.title}</p>
                <p className="message-date">{new Date(message.date).toLocaleDateString()}</p>
                <p className="message-description">{message.description}</p>
              </div>
            ))}
            {hasMoreMessages && !showAll && (
              <button
                className="btn btn-link show-more-btn"
                onClick={() => setShowAll(true)}
              >
                הצג עוד הודעות
              </button>
            )}
          </div>
        );
      }

      async function fetchData() {

        const requiredPromises = [];
        const otherPromises = [];

        if (requiredKeys.includes("status")) {
          requiredPromises.push(getStatus());
        } else {
          otherPromises.push(getStatus());
        }

        if (requiredKeys.includes("classifications")) {
          requiredPromises.push(getClassifications());
        } else {
          otherPromises.push(getClassifications());
        }

        if (requiredKeys.includes("fields")) {
          requiredPromises.push(getFields());
        } else {
          otherPromises.push(getFields());
        }

        // if (requiredKeys.includes("safeTime")) {
        //   requiredPromises.push(getSafeTime());
        // } else {
        //   otherPromises.push(getSafeTime());
        // }

        if (requiredKeys.includes("materials")) {
          requiredPromises.push(fetchMaterials());
        } else {
          otherPromises.push(fetchMaterials());
        }

        if (requiredKeys.includes("orefCitiesData")) {
          requiredPromises.push(fetchOrefCities());
        } else {
          otherPromises.push(fetchOrefCities());
        }

        if (requiredKeys.includes("transportTypes")) {
          requiredPromises.push(fetchTransportTypes());
        } else {
          otherPromises.push(fetchTransportTypes());
        }

        if (requiredKeys.includes("permitRequestTypes")) {
          requiredPromises.push(fetchPermitRequestTypes());
        } else {
          otherPromises.push(fetchPermitRequestTypes());
        }

        if (requiredKeys.includes("requiredDocuments")) {
          requiredPromises.push(fetchRequiredDocuments());
        } else {
          otherPromises.push(fetchRequiredDocuments());
        }

        try {
          await Promise.all(requiredPromises);
          setDataLoaded(true);
        } catch (error) {
          console.error("Error in required data:", error);
          // אפשר לטפל בזה בצורה מותאמת—למשל להציג הודעה למשתמש
        }

        Promise.all(otherPromises).catch(error => console.error("Error in non-required data:", error));
      }

      React.useEffect(() => {
        fetchData();
      }, []);

      return null
    }

    function MyHeaderWrapper({ setShowMobileMsgModal, setShowMobileUserMenu, setCurrentPage, showMobileUserMenu }) {
    const [isMobile, setIsMobile] = React.useState(mobileCheck());

    React.useEffect(() => {
      const handleResize = () => setIsMobile(mobileCheck());
      window.addEventListener("resize", handleResize);
      return () => window.removeEventListener("resize", handleResize);
    }, []);

    return isMobile
      ? <MobileHeader
          setShowMobileMsgModal={setShowMobileMsgModal}
          setShowMobileUserMenu={setShowMobileUserMenu}
          showMobileUserMenu={showMobileUserMenu}
          setCurrentPage={setCurrentPage}

        />
      : <MyToolbar setCurrentPage={setCurrentPage} />;
  }

      function InnerDropDown({ generalLogOut }) {
        return (
          <ul className='dropdown-menu dropdown-menu-end' id="disconnected-drop">
            <li>
              <a className="dropdown-item" id="user-profile" href="/UserProfile/" aria-label="הגדרות משתמש" aria-roledescription="link" title="הגדרות משתמש">
                הגדרות משתמש
              </a>
              <a className="dropdown-item" id="disconnected" aria-label="התנתק" aria-roledescription="link" title="התנתק" onClick={generalLogOut}>
                התנתק
              </a>
            </li>
          </ul>
        )
      }

    function MobileHeader({ setShowMobileMsgModal, setShowMobileUserMenu, setCurrentPage, showMobileUserMenu  }) {
      return (
        <header className="mobile-header">
          <div className="header-content">
            <div className="right-side" onClick={() => {  window.location.href ="/" }}>
              <img src="/hazard-logo.png" className="icon-circle" alt="hazard" />
              <img src="/pakar-logo.png" className="icon-circle" alt="pakar" />
              <span className="header-title">מרכז חומרים מסוכנים</span>
            </div>
            <div className="left-side">
              <div className="icon-wrapper mail" onClick={() => setShowMobileMsgModal(true)}>
                <img src="/messages-icon.png" className="icon-circle" alt="msg" />
                <span className="notification-dot"></span>
              </div>
              <div className="icon-wrapper" data-bs-toggle='dropdown' onClick={() => setShowMobileUserMenu(true)}>
                <img src="/user-icon.png" className="icon-circle" alt="user" />
              </div>
              <ReactBootstrap.Offcanvas show={showMobileUserMenu} onHide={() => setShowMobileUserMenu(false)} placement="end">
                <ReactBootstrap.Offcanvas.Body>
                  <div className="btn-close-custom">
                  <button
                    type="button"
                    aria-label="Close"
                    onClick={() => setShowMobileUserMenu(false)}
                  >
                  <img src="/close-icon.png" alt="x" />
                  </button>
                </div>
                  <InnerDropDown generalLogOut={generalLogOut} />
                </ReactBootstrap.Offcanvas.Body>
              </ReactBootstrap.Offcanvas>
            </div>
          </div>
        </header>
      )
    }

    const Loader = ({ className = "ms-2", size = "md", centered = false, opacity = 1 }) => {
      const loaderClass = `loader ${centered ? "d-flex justify-content-center my-3" : className}`;

      return (
        <div className={loaderClass}>
          <ReactBootstrap.Spinner animation="border" role="status" size={size}>
            <span className="visually-hidden">Loading...</span>
          </ReactBootstrap.Spinner>
        </div>
      );
    };

        function GoToNewEditor() {
            var editCmsUrlSegment = "EditInCms";
            var currentUrl = window.location.href;
            if (currentUrl.indexOf('?') > -1) {
                var urlSegments = currentUrl.split("?");
                window.location.href = window.location.origin + '/' + editCmsUrlSegment + window.location.pathname + '?' + urlSegments[1];
            }
            else {
                window.location.href = window.location.origin + '/' + editCmsUrlSegment + window.location.pathname;
            }
        }
    </script>
